	<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">2003 BDO World Darts Championship</h1>
	
	<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
		<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div>
		<div id="contentSub"></div>
		
		
		
		<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>
		<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>
		<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">

</p>

<td style="text-align:right"><a href="/wiki/2004_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="2004 BDO World Darts Championship">2004</a>»</td>
</tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p>The <b>2003 BDO World Darts Championship</b> was a professional <a href="/wiki/Darts" title="Darts">darts</a> tournament held from 4 to 12 January 2003 at the <a href="/wiki/Lakeside_Leisure_Complex" title="Lakeside Leisure Complex">Lakeside Country Club</a> in <a href="/wiki/Frimley_Green" title="Frimley Green">Frimley Green</a>, <a href="/wiki/Surrey" title="Surrey">Surrey</a>. It was the 26th staging of the <a href="/wiki/BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="BDO World Darts Championship">competition</a> since the <a href="/wiki/1978_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1978 BDO World Darts Championship">1978 edition</a> and the 18th time it took place at the Lakeside Country Club. The tournament was the first of 14 <a href="/wiki/British_Darts_Organisation" title="British Darts Organisation">British Darts Organisation</a> (BDO) tournaments in 2003. The competition was broadcast by the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a> and was sponsored by the cigarette company <a href="/wiki/Embassy_(cigarette)" title="Embassy (cigarette)">Embassy</a>.
</p><p>Two-time world champion <a href="/wiki/Raymond_van_Barneveld" title="Raymond van Barneveld">Raymond van Barneveld</a> defeated <a href="/wiki/Ritchie_Davies" title="Ritchie Davies">Ritchie Davies</a> six <a href="/wiki/Set_(darts)" title="Set (darts)">sets</a> to three (6–3) in the final. He joined <a href="/wiki/Eric_Bristow" title="Eric Bristow">Eric Bristow</a> and <a href="/wiki/John_Lowe" title="John Lowe">John Lowe</a> as the third player to win three or more BDO world titles in their career. Van Barneveld defeated <a href="/wiki/Matt_Clark_(darts_player)" title="Matt Clark (darts player)">Matt Clark</a>, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=John_Burton_(darts_player)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="John Burton (darts player) (page does not exist)">John Burton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Erik_Clarys" title="Erik Clarys">Erik Clarys</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mervyn_King_(darts_player)" title="Mervyn King (darts player)">Mervyn King</a> on his way to reaching the final. Clarys achieved a 170 <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_darts#Checkout" title="Glossary of darts">checkout</a>, the highest of the tournament, in the final set of his quarter-final round match against Van Barneveld. A women's world championship was held for the third time. It was won by <a href="/wiki/Trina_Gulliver" title="Trina Gulliver">Trina Gulliver</a> for the third consecutive year, defeating <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dawn_Standley&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dawn Standley (page does not exist)">Dawn Standley</a> 2–1 in the quarter-final, <a href="/wiki/Whitewash_(sport)" title="Whitewash (sport)">whitewashing</a> <a href="/wiki/Mieke_de_Boer" title="Mieke de Boer">Mieke de Boer</a> 2–0 in the semi-final and beating <a href="/wiki/Anne_Kirk" title="Anne Kirk">Anne Kirk</a> 2–1 in the final.
</p>

<h2><span id="Men.27s_tournament"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Men's_tournament">Men's tournament</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Men's tournament">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Background">Background</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Background">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/British_Darts_Organisation" title="British Darts Organisation">British Darts Organisation</a> (BDO) was formed in 1973 by the managing director <a href="/wiki/Olly_Croft" title="Olly Croft">Olly Croft</a>; the BDO World Darts Championship was first held in 1978.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup> It is one of two <a href="/wiki/World_championship" title="World championship">world championships</a> in the game of <a href="/wiki/Darts" title="Darts">darts</a>: the other being the <a href="/wiki/PDC_World_Darts_Championship" title="PDC World Darts Championship">PDC World Darts Championship</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> The 2003 tournament was held between 4 and 12 January in <a href="/wiki/Frimley_Green" title="Frimley Green">Frimley Green</a>, <a href="/wiki/Surrey" title="Surrey">Surrey</a> and was the first of 14 BDO-sanctioned events that year.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TDEDarts_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-TDEDarts-4">[4]</a></sup> It was the 26th edition of the tournament and featured a 32-player main draw that was played at the <a href="/wiki/Lakeside_Leisure_Complex" title="Lakeside Leisure Complex">Lakeside Country Club</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-E2003Darts_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-E2003Darts-5">[5]</a></sup>
</p><p>27 players automatically qualified for the main draw with the top 8 <a href="/wiki/Seed_(sports)" title="Seed (sports)">seeded</a> according to their final position in the BDO rankings. The tournament's defending champion and world number one <a href="/wiki/Tony_David" title="Tony David">Tony David</a> was seeded first and <a href="/wiki/Raymond_van_Barneveld" title="Raymond van Barneveld">Raymond van Barneveld</a> was seeded second.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TDEDarts_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-TDEDarts-4">[4]</a></sup> The remaining five places were decided via an international play-off round that was held at the <a href="/wiki/Bridlington_Spa" title="Bridlington Spa">Bridlington Spa</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bridlington" title="Bridlington">Bridlington</a> on 31 October 2002.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TDEDarts_4-2"><a href="#cite_note-TDEDarts-4">[4]</a></sup> <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=John_Burton_(darts_player)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="John Burton (darts player) (page does not exist)">John Burton</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dennis_Harbour" title="Dennis Harbour">Dennis Harbour</a>. <a href="/wiki/Martin_Phillips_(darts_player)" title="Martin Phillips (darts player)">Martin Phillips</a>, <a href="/wiki/Brian_Buur" title="Brian Buur">Brian Sorensen</a> and <a href="/wiki/Robert_Wagner_(darts_player)" title="Robert Wagner (darts player)">Robert Wagner</a> were the five players who progressed from the qualifying round to the main draw.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PlayOffResults_6-0"><a href="#cite_note-PlayOffResults-6">[6]</a></sup> The number of <a href="/wiki/Set_(darts)" title="Set (darts)">sets</a> needed to win a match increased from five in the first and second rounds to nine in the quarter and semi-finals, leading up to the final which was played as best-of-11 frames.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup> Sponsored by the cigarette brand <a href="/wiki/Embassy_(cigarette)" title="Embassy (cigarette)">Embassy</a>,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DDatabase2003Men_8-0"><a href="#cite_note-DDatabase2003Men-8">[8]</a></sup> it had a total prize fund of £205,000,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes_9-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes-9">[9]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7803PrizeMoney_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-7803PrizeMoney-10">[10]</a></sup> and was broadcast in the United Kingdom on the <a href="/wiki/BBC" title="BBC">BBC</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DDatabase2003Men_8-1"><a href="#cite_note-DDatabase2003Men-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the lead up to the 2002 BDO world championship, David was seen by <i><a href="/wiki/The_Times" title="The Times">The Times</a></i> correspondent Mel Webb as the favourite to retain his title due to his performances throughout the 2002 season.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TimesPreview_11-0"><a href="#cite_note-TimesPreview-11">[11]</a></sup> Eight top seeds <a href="/wiki/John_Lowe" title="John Lowe">John Lowe</a> (<a href="/wiki/1979_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1979 BDO World Darts Championship">1979</a>), <a href="/wiki/Eric_Bristow" title="Eric Bristow">Eric Bristow</a> (<a href="/wiki/1981_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1981 BDO World Darts Championship">1981</a>, <a href="/wiki/1984_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1984 BDO World Darts Championship">1984</a>, <a href="/wiki/1985_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1985 BDO World Darts Championship">1985</a> and <a href="/wiki/1986_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1986 BDO World Darts Championship">1986</a>), <a href="/wiki/Bob_Anderson_(darts_player)" title="Bob Anderson (darts player)">Bob Anderson</a> (<a href="/wiki/1988_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1988 BDO World Darts Championship">1988</a>), <a href="/wiki/Phil_Taylor_(darts_player)" title="Phil Taylor (darts player)">Phil Taylor</a> (<a href="/wiki/1992_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1992 BDO World Darts Championship">1992</a>) and Van Barneveld (<a href="/wiki/1998_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1998 BDO World Darts Championship">1998</a> and <a href="/wiki/1999_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="1999 BDO World Darts Championship">1999</a>) had won the competition beforehand.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCPreview_12-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCPreview-12">[12]</a></sup> Conversely, <i><a href="/wiki/Racing_Post" title="Racing Post">The Racing Post</a></i>'s Steve Davies reported bookmakers considered Van Barneveld the most likely player to win the tournament, which would be his third BDO world championship victory.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TRPPreview_13-0"><a href="#cite_note-TRPPreview-13">[13]</a></sup> Embassy Darts guest writer Marcus Stead opined the progress of <a href="/wiki/John_Walton_(darts_player)" title="John Walton (darts player)">John Walton</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2001_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="2001 BDO World Darts Championship">2001 champion</a>, would be observed carefully.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14"><a href="#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Round_1">Round 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Round 1">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The draw for the first round of the championship was conducted by <a href="/wiki/Peter_Ebdon" title="Peter Ebdon">Peter Ebdon</a>, the <a href="/wiki/2002_World_Snooker_Championship" title="2002 World Snooker Championship">2002 world snooker champion</a>, and the two-time women's darts champion <a href="/wiki/Trina_Gulliver" title="Trina Gulliver">Trina Gulliver</a> at the Bridlington Spa on 3 November 2002. It was televised live on the BBC sport programme <i><a href="/wiki/Grandstand_(TV_programme)" title="Grandstand (TV programme)">Sunday Grandstand</a></i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-R1Draw_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-R1Draw-15">[15]</a></sup> The first round of the competition, in which 32 players participated, took place from 4 to 6 January and was held to the best-of-five sets.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes_9-1"><a href="#cite_note-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes-9">[9]</a></sup>
</p><p>In this round <a href="/wiki/Vincent_van_der_Voort" title="Vincent van der Voort">Vincent van der Voort</a> defeated <a href="/wiki/Jarkko_Komula" title="Jarkko Komula">Jarkko Komula</a> 3–1. Komula moved 2–0 ahead in the first set until Van Der Voort produced an 11-dart finish to win set one. Van Der Voort overcame a challenge from Komula to finish the match with a 117 <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_darts#C" title="Glossary of darts">checkout</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay1_16-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay1-16">[16]</a></sup> David, who suffers from the blood-clotting disorder <a href="/wiki/Haemophilia" title="Haemophilia">haemophilia</a>, lost the first set in his match against Sorensen (from a 109 checkout) due to several dart throws ending outside the board's targets before winning three sets in a row to claim a 3–1 victory; David won five consecutive <a href="/wiki/Leg_(darts)" title="Leg (darts)">legs</a> to take the lead.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WOSDay1_17-0"><a href="#cite_note-WOSDay1-17">[17]</a></sup> Against Phillips, Walton claimed set one before Phillips claimed six successive legs to lead 2–1. Two double one ring finishes gave Walton the fourth set and took the fifth to win 3–2.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay1_16-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay1-16">[16]</a></sup> Walton said he had received treatment for a <a href="/wiki/Nerve_compression_syndrome" title="Nerve compression syndrome">trapped nerve</a> in his neck before the match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WOSDay1_17-1"><a href="#cite_note-WOSDay1-17">[17]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Ritchie_Davies" title="Ritchie Davies">Ritchie Davies</a>, in his seventh appearance in a row at the tournament, defeated <a href="/wiki/Albertino_Essers" title="Albertino Essers">Albertino Essers</a> 3–1, a match which saw Davies claim the opening set unchallenged. <a href="/wiki/Gary_Anderson_(darts_player)" title="Gary Anderson (darts player)">Gary Anderson</a> prevailed 3–2 over <a href="/wiki/Peter_Johnstone_(darts_player)" title="Peter Johnstone (darts player)">Peter Johnstone</a> in a narrowly-fought match. Anderson converted a 2–0 deficit to win the first set 3–2. He and Johnstone twice equalled the game before Anderson won three legs in a row to win.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay1_16-2"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay1-16">[16]</a></sup> Four-time semi-finalist <a href="/wiki/Andy_Fordham" title="Andy Fordham">Andy Fordham</a> complied high scores and struck the <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_darts#D" title="Glossary of darts">double rings</a> to <a href="/wiki/Whitewash_(sport)" title="Whitewash (sport)">whitewash</a> <a href="/wiki/Stefan_Nagy" title="Stefan Nagy">Stefan Nagy</a> 3–0.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay1_16-3"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay1-16">[16]</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Bob_Taylor_(darts_player)" title="Bob Taylor (darts player)">Bob Taylor</a> progressed past the first round for the second year in a row with a 3–0 whitewash of <a href="/wiki/Peter_Hunt_(darts_player)" title="Peter Hunt (darts player)">Peter Hunt</a> with set victories of 3–2 and 3–1 (x2). In both their maiden television appearance, <a href="/wiki/Darryl_Fitton" title="Darryl Fitton">Darryl Fitton</a> defeated Burton 3–1 with set victories of 3–0, 3–2 and 3–1.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCDay2_18-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDay2-18">[18]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Martin_Adams" title="Martin Adams">Martin Adams</a>, the number four seed and <a href="/wiki/England_Darts_Organisation" title="England Darts Organisation">England captain</a> who competed at the tournament for the tenth time,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndyDay2_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-IndyDay2-19">[19]</a></sup> claimed the opening set against <a href="/wiki/Co_Stomp%C3%A9" title="Co Stompé">Co Stompé</a>. He beat Stompé in the second set and took a 3–1 victory with a 138 checkout.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCDay2_18-1"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDay2-18">[18]</a></sup> Wagner won the opening set against <a href="/wiki/Gary_Robson_(darts_player)" title="Gary Robson (darts player)">Gary Robson</a> 3–2 before Robson won the following set after Wagner missed multiple chances to hit the double ten ring. Wagner won two more sets coupled with six consecutive legs to win 3–1.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay2_20-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay2-20">[20]</a></sup> In the match between Van Barneveld and <a href="/wiki/Matt_Clark_(darts_player)" title="Matt Clark (darts player)">Matt Clark</a>, the latter began with a <a href="/wiki/Glossary_of_darts#Maximum" title="Glossary of darts">maximum score</a> (180) before the former took the first set. He then claimed six legs in a row to secure a 3–1 victory.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndyDay2_19-1"><a href="#cite_note-IndyDay2-19">[19]</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Erik_Clarys" title="Erik Clarys">Erik Clarys</a> defeated the seventh seed <a href="/wiki/Tony_Eccles" title="Tony Eccles">Tony Eccles</a> 3–1 after he overcame a minor challenge from Eccles in set three.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndyDay2_19-2"><a href="#cite_note-IndyDay2-19">[19]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay2_20-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay2-20">[20]</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Shaun_Greatbatch" title="Shaun Greatbatch">Shaun Greatbatch</a> had a sub-par performance against <a href="/wiki/Colin_Monk" title="Colin Monk">Colin Monk</a> and was whitewashed 3–0; Greatbatch was able to force the second set to conclude with a final leg decider before he missed the double rings in the following set.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCDay3_21-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDay3-21">[21]</a></sup> Sixth seed <a href="/wiki/Tony_O%27Shea" title="Tony O'Shea">Tony O'Shea</a> edged out the <a href="/wiki/2000_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="2000 BDO World Darts Championship">2000 champion</a> <a href="/wiki/Ted_Hankey" title="Ted Hankey">Ted Hankey</a> 3–2 in a closely-contested match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22"><a href="#cite_note-22">[22]</a></sup> Hankey won the first set unchallenged before a 118 checkout gave O'Shea the next set. The score was level until O'Shea defeated Hankey on a finish to the double 16 ring.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCDay3_21-1"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDay3-21">[21]</a></sup> Another closely-contested game occurred when Harbour defeated teenager <a href="/wiki/James_Wade" title="James Wade">James Wade</a> 3–2. Coming from 2–1 behind Harbour produced checkouts of 145, 115 and 60 in the sixth set to go through to the next round after Wade was unable to convert ten opportunities to win the match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23"><a href="#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> The final match of the first round was played between the number three seed <a href="/wiki/Mervyn_King_(darts_player)" title="Mervyn King (darts player)">Mervyn King</a> and <a href="/wiki/Steve_Coote" title="Steve Coote">Steve Coote</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-1"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup> After King compiled a 138 checkout, Coote won the first set 3–2 with a finish of 101 points. King moved in front by taking sets two and three by 3–1. A 116 checkout allowed King to win 3–1.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24"><a href="#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Round_2">Round 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Round 2">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Martin_Adams_2012.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="299" data-file-width="356" decoding="async" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Martin_Adams_2012.jpg/170px-Martin_Adams_2012.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Martin_Adams_2012.jpg/255px-Martin_Adams_2012.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/42/Martin_Adams_2012.jpg/340px-Martin_Adams_2012.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Martin_Adams_2012.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Martin_Adams" title="Martin Adams">Martin Adams</a> <i>(pictured in 2012)</i> was eliminated in the second-round of the competition</div></div></div>
<p>The second round was held from 7 to 8 January.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-2"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup> The first second round match, which was played between Adams and Taylor,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-3"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup> began with Adams winning the five-leg first set on the double 20 ring and led by two legs in set two. Taylor equalled the score with a 116 checkout and won the third set 3–1. After Adams could not hit the bullseye ring Taylor claimed a 3–1 victory,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25"><a href="#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup> and became the first player to go through to the quarter-finals.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay4_26-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay4-26">[26]</a></sup> David came from one set behind Van Der Voort early on to win 3–1 with a 114 checkout and a finish of 99 points, saying afterwards: "I was a bit slow coming out in the first set but I picked it up and I'm very happy with how I played."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27"><a href="#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> Davies whitewashed Walton 3–0 with two finishes of twelve darts each and finished on the double 20 ring; Walton was non-competitive missed multiple opportunities to strike a double ring. In the match between Anderson and Fordham, Anderson won the first set on the <a href="/wiki/Bullseye_(target)" title="Bullseye (target)">bullseye ring</a> to which Fordham replied by winning three legs in a row without reply to level the score. Anderson then claimed the next two sets and finished on the double six ring for a 3–1 victory.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay4_26-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay4-26">[26]</a></sup>
</p><p>Van Barneveld whitewashed Burton 3–0 with a finish that took twelve dart throws; Burton won a single leg in each of the three sets played as he could not mount a challenge to Van Barneveld during the game.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndyDay5_28-0"><a href="#cite_note-IndyDay5-28">[28]</a></sup> Clarys came from two legs behind Wagner to win a tightly-contested first set 3–2 and went on whitewash his opponent 3–0.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCDay5_29-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDay5-29">[29]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay5_30-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay5-30">[30]</a></sup> Monk overcame O'Shea 3–2 in a narrowly fought match that the press positively reviewed.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndyDay5_28-1"><a href="#cite_note-IndyDay5-28">[28]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCDay5_29-1"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDay5-29">[29]</a></sup> Both players tied at 2–2 and the match concluded with a final set decider. The score went to 5–5 when the <a href="/wiki/Referee" title="Referee">referee</a> called for a <a href="/wiki/Sudden_death_(sport)" title="Sudden death (sport)">sudden death</a> leg, which Monk won with a 102 checkout through striking the treble 20, single 10 and double 16 rings.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay5_30-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay5-30">[30]</a></sup> Monk said he was exhausted after the match and O'Shea credited his opponent for his form.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCDay5_29-2"><a href="#cite_note-BBCDay5-29">[29]</a></sup> In the final second round match Harbour was defeated 3–1 by King. Two 12 dart finishes and three maximum scores won King set one. King prevented Harbour from winning the second by hitting the double eight ring. Harbour took the third set before King won the match in the fourth.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay5_30-2"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay5-30">[30]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quarter-finals">Quarter-finals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Quarter-finals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The four quarter-finals were played to the best-of-nine sets between 9 and 10 January.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-4"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup> Davies averaged 32.73 per dart thrown in whitewashing David 5–0. He won the opening two sets from scores of 3–0 and 3–2. Davies further extended his lead through dart throw accuracy and after David could not strike the double 20 ring in the third set. After the mid-session interval, both players tied the fifth set 2–2 until Davies achieved a 121 checkout to earn the competition's first semi-final berth.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay6_31-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay6-31">[31]</a></sup> He entered the semi-finals of the championship for the first time in his seventh appearance.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32"><a href="#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> David said after his match Davies had outperformed him and the latter expressed his surprise he was able to whitewash his opponent.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33"><a href="#cite_note-33">[33]</a></sup> Another whitewash occurred when Taylor was defeated 0–5 by Anderson in an all-Scottish fixture. He compiled checkouts of 161 and 140 and a finish that took 13 dart throws to achieve en route to claiming the match victory.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay6_31-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay6-31">[31]</a></sup> Anderson said of his form afterwards: "I thought I'd win tonight but I thought it would be a lot closer than that. I was fine against Andy Fordham but I felt a little bit nervous tonight. However, I'm through and I've got nothing to lose."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34"><a href="#cite_note-34">[34]</a></sup>
</p><p>In the other quarter-finals Van Barneveld achieved a three-dart throw average of 100.83 and a finish percentage of 59.25 in his 5–1 defeat of Clarys.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35"><a href="#cite_note-35">[35]</a></sup> The match included a tournament-high checkout of 170 from Clarys in the final set.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ScotsmanClarysBarneveld_36-0"><a href="#cite_note-ScotsmanClarysBarneveld-36">[36]</a></sup> Van Barneveld won the first two sets and Clarys took the third 3–1. Van Barneveld produced a 124 checkout in set four to restore a two set advantage.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ScotsmanClarysBarneveld_36-1"><a href="#cite_note-ScotsmanClarysBarneveld-36">[36]</a></sup> He then took the following two sets 3–0 and 3–2 to progress to the semi-finals.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay7_37-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay7-37">[37]</a></sup> King whitewashed Monk 5–0 in a repeat of their semi-final match from the 2002 tournament. Both players shared the opening four legs of the first set before King struck the double six ring to take an advantage he retained for the rest of the game to claim the last semi-final berth.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay7_37-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay7-37">[37]</a></sup> He commented on what he needed to defeat Van Barneveld, "I've got to be looking for a 99 to 100 average against Raymond. As you all know, it's not beyond me. But I'm just looking for the win at the end of day, because the Embassy is what you play for."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-38"><a href="#cite_note-38">[38]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Semi-finals">Semi-finals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Semi-finals">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gary_Anderson_(Exeter_2016).jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2689" data-file-width="2151" decoding="async" height="213" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Gary_Anderson_%28Exeter_2016%29.jpg/170px-Gary_Anderson_%28Exeter_2016%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Gary_Anderson_%28Exeter_2016%29.jpg/255px-Gary_Anderson_%28Exeter_2016%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Gary_Anderson_%28Exeter_2016%29.jpg/340px-Gary_Anderson_%28Exeter_2016%29.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Gary_Anderson_(Exeter_2016).jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Gary_Anderson_(darts_player)" title="Gary Anderson (darts player)">Gary Anderson</a> <i>(pictured in 2016)</i> reached the semi-finals of the tournament</div></div></div>
<p>Both of the semi-finals were played on 11 January.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-5"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup> Davies defeated Anderson 5–2 to enter the final.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WOSSFDaviesAnderson_39-0"><a href="#cite_note-WOSSFDaviesAnderson-39">[39]</a></sup> The two players began the match by sharing the first two sets each. Davies subsequently produced a 140 checkout to move in front and he further extended his advantage by winning the fourth set with a finish on the double five ring. After the mid-session interval Anderson threw twenty-eight darts and achieved a checkout that saw him hit the triple 19 and double 12 rings to claim set five. Davies responded to Anderson's form by claiming the next set 3–2; a fifteen-dart finish and Davies throwing a dart onto the double ten ring in the eighth set secured him the match victory.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay8_40-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay8-40">[40]</a></sup> Davies said he began slower than before and was eager to participate in the final, "If anyone would have told me at the start of the week that I would be in the final, I'd have laughed. But I've got nothing to lose in this tournament. I've just come here to do as well as I can."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WOSSFDaviesAnderson_39-1"><a href="#cite_note-WOSSFDaviesAnderson-39">[39]</a></sup>
</p><p>The other semi-final game saw Van Barneveld enter the final of the championship with a 5–2 defeat of King and requited a loss to his opponent from the 2002 competition.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IESFKingVanBarneveld_41-0"><a href="#cite_note-IESFKingVanBarneveld-41">[41]</a></sup> The first four legs of the first set were shared by both players and went to a fifth leg Van Barneveld won on the double eight ring. Van Barneveld produced a 110 checkout and won two more sets to lead by two sets.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IESFKingVanBarneveld_41-1"><a href="#cite_note-IESFKingVanBarneveld-41">[41]</a></sup> Both players could not attain a <a href="/wiki/Nine-dart_finish" title="Nine-dart finish">nine-dart finish</a> in the first leg of set three: King missed the triple 20 ring and Van Barneveld the triple 19 ring on his eighth throw. Van Barneveld converted two twelve-dart finishes to lead 3–0. King then clinched two sets in a row to be 3–2 behind before Van Barneveld achieved a finish on the double eight ring and a 161 checkout to win the match.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsDay8_40-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsDay8-40">[40]</a></sup> After the game, King inculpated his defeat to the trajectory of his darts being affected by an <a href="/wiki/Air_conditioning" title="Air conditioning">air conditioning system</a> not being switched off by the tournament organisers, something the BDO denied.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KingAirCon_42-0"><a href="#cite_note-KingAirCon-42">[42]</a></sup> He commented: "Under the conditions, I thought I played exceptionally well - but to beat a player like Raymond, everything has to be right and fair."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-KingAirCon_42-1"><a href="#cite_note-KingAirCon-42">[42]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final">Final</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Final">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="600" data-file-width="600" decoding="async" height="170" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg/170px-Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg/255px-Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg/340px-Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg 2x" width="170"/></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Raymond_van_Barneveld.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Raymond_van_Barneveld" title="Raymond van Barneveld">Raymond van Barneveld</a> <i>(pictured in 2006)</i> defeated <a href="/wiki/Ritchie_Davies" title="Ritchie Davies">Ritchie Davies</a> to win his third BDO world championship.</div></div></div>
<p>The final played between Davies and Van Barneveld on 12 January was held to the best-of-11 sets.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-6"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup> Both players missed hitting the double rings before Van Barneveld produced a 132 checkout with a finish on the double one ring to take the first set 3–1 after twelve dart throws in leg four. He further extended his lead to 4–0 with three consecutive scorelines of 3–2 that was achieved from respective finishes on the double 11 ring in the second set, a 116 checkout in the third and throwing eleven darts in the final leg of the fourth set.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndyFinal_43-0"><a href="#cite_note-IndyFinal-43">[43]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TimesFinal_44-0"><a href="#cite_note-TimesFinal-44">[44]</a></sup> Finishes on the double 16 and 11 rings and a 121 checkout secured Davies the fifth set 3–1 and followed with a tightly-fought fifth set 3–2. During the seventh set Davies won his third successive set from finishes on the double 20 ring, achieving a 98 checkout and hitting the double 10 ring. The eighth set was taken 3–2 by Van Barneveld from two checkouts of 76 points and striking the double 18 ring in its fifth leg. Davies claimed the first leg of set nine after Van Barneveld was unable to convert a 84 finish. Van Barneveld then made finishes of 96 and 72 points to win the set 3–1, the match 6–3 and the tournament.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCSetbySet_45-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCSetbySet-45">[45]</a></sup>
</p><p>Van Barneveld took his third BDO world championship after he had won the tournament in 1998 and 1999.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IndyFinal_43-1"><a href="#cite_note-IndyFinal-43">[43]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TimesFinal_44-1"><a href="#cite_note-TimesFinal-44">[44]</a></sup> He became the third player after Eric Bristow and John Lowe to win three or more BDO world titles,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCRVBWin_46-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCRVBWin-46">[46]</a></sup> and earned £50,000 for the win.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes_9-2"><a href="#cite_note-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes-9">[9]</a></sup> Van Barneveld commented on his victory: "When you the win the title for the first time it's very good. After 2000 when I lost in the first round I did not believe in myself. I've had to work hard to get on this level again. Mentally, the fight came back in my life and I started to believe in myself again."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCRVBWin_46-1"><a href="#cite_note-BBCRVBWin-46">[46]</a></sup> Davies said he would return to participate the championship for the <a href="/wiki/2004_BDO_World_Darts_Championship" title="2004 BDO World Darts Championship">2004 edition</a> and admitted losing the opening four sets altered his strategy: "I knew with such a long format I had time to settle down but I gave Raymond too many chances. I was very nervous and, at the start, the darts just would not seem to fall the way they have been doing all week. I was trying and trying but Raymond was always coming up with the big score when he needed it. It is hard to play Raymond because once he gets into a rhythm it is very difficult to stop him. I hit too many single 20s tonight which was also disappointing."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SWEDavies_47-0"><a href="#cite_note-SWEDavies-47">[47]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id="Women.27s_tournament"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Women's_tournament">Women's tournament</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Women's tournament">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The BDO women's world championship was the third edition of the tournament,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsWomen_48-0"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsWomen-48">[48]</a></sup> and took place from 4 to 11 January at the Lakeside Country Club, Frimley Green, Surrey.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCallerWomen_49-0"><a href="#cite_note-MCallerWomen-49">[49]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCWomenResults_50-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWomenResults-50">[50]</a></sup> Four players automatically qualified for the main draw and were seeded according to their final position in the BDO rankings. <a href="/wiki/Francis_Hoenselaar" title="Francis Hoenselaar">Francis Hoenselaar</a> was seeded first and the competition's defending champion Trina Gulliver  was the second seed. <a href="/wiki/Mieke_de_Boer" title="Mieke de Boer">Mieke de Boer</a> was seeded third and the final seed was <a href="/wiki/Anne_Kirk" title="Anne Kirk">Anne Kirk</a>. <a href="/wiki/Karin_Krappen" title="Karin Krappen">Karin Krappen</a> was the only automatic non-seeded participant. The remaining three places were decided via an international play-off round held at the Bridlington Spa, Bridlington on 31 October 2002. <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Linda_Rogers-Pickett&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Linda Rogers-Pickett (page does not exist)">Linda Rogers-Pickett</a>, <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Dawn_Standley&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Dawn Standley (page does not exist)">Dawn Standley</a> and <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Gaynor_Williams&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Gaynor Williams (page does not exist)">Gaynor Williams</a> were the trio who advanced from qualifying to the main draw.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TDEDarts_4-3"><a href="#cite_note-TDEDarts-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-E2003Darts_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-E2003Darts-5">[5]</a></sup> All matches were played to the best-of-three sets.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCallerWomen_49-1"><a href="#cite_note-MCallerWomen-49">[49]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCWomenResults_50-1"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWomenResults-50">[50]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Quarter-finals_to_the_final">Quarter-finals to the final</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Quarter-finals to the final">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The four quarter-finals took place between 4 and 5 January.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCallerWomen_49-2"><a href="#cite_note-MCallerWomen-49">[49]</a></sup> Pre-tournament favourite Hoensellar and Krappen played the first quarter-final match. Krappen took the first set 3-0 before Hoensellar won the match 2–1 with set victories of 3–0 and 3–1. Kirk and Williams tied at 2–2 in the first set of their match before Kirk took the fifth leg to claim it. Kirk then won three legs in a row to whitewash Williams 2–0. Gulliver defeated Standley 2–1. Gulliver won the first set 3–0 after Standley was unable to convert a double ring finish. Standley won the next set 3–1 before Gulliver completed the victory by claiming sets three. The final quarter-final match saw De Boer whitewash Rogers-Pickett 2–0; Rogers-Pickett tied the second set 2–2 before De Boer struck the double eight ring to win.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsWomen_48-1"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsWomen-48">[48]</a></sup>
</p><p>Both of the semi-finals were held on 9 January.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCWomenResults_50-2"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWomenResults-50">[50]</a></sup> Kirk took a 2–0 lead over Hoenselaar before the latter levelled the scoreline. Kirk then won the first set and Hoensellar commenced the second by claiming its first leg. Kirk claimed three consecutive legs to win 2–0 and earn a berth in the final. The other semi-final match saw Gulliver whitewash De Boer 2–0. De Boer took the match's first leg to which Gulliver compiled high scores for three successive leg victories and win the first set. Gulliver took set two to secure the second final berth.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsWomen_48-2"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsWomen-48">[48]</a></sup>
</p><p>The final was played between Gulliver and Kirk on 11 January.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCallerWomen_49-3"><a href="#cite_note-MCallerWomen-49">[49]</a></sup> Gulliver clinched the first leg on the double nine ring and followed with two more legs to win the first set 3–0.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RAGulliver_51-0"><a href="#cite_note-RAGulliver-51">[51]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCWomensFinal_52-0"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWomensFinal-52">[52]</a></sup> Kirk claimed the first two legs of the second set after Gulliver was unable to attain a 121 checkout after she missed the bullseye ring.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-EDartsWomen_48-3"><a href="#cite_note-EDartsWomen-48">[48]</a></sup> Gulliver subsequently took the next two legs to equal the scoreline. In the fifth leg Gulliver compiled a maximum score and won her third BDO world championship from a 93 checkout, which she completed on the double twelve ring.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCWomensFinal_52-1"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWomensFinal-52">[52]</a></sup> She said of her achievement, "It hasn't really sunk in yet, but when I think about it, I just think wow! It's unbelievable. Mine's still the only name on the trophy and I never want to give it back! I had a lot of pressure on me, admittedly a lot of it I'd put on myself, but I was able to handle it and hold it together."<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RAGulliver_51-1"><a href="#cite_note-RAGulliver-51">[51]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Prize_fund">Prize fund</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Prize fund">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Draw">Draw</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Draw">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Men.27s_draw"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Men's_draw">Men's draw</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Men's draw">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Numbers given to the left of players' names show the seedings for the top eight players in the men's tournament. The five qualifiers are indicated by a (Q). The figures in brackets to the right of a competitor's name state their three-dart finishing averages in a match. Players in bold denote match winners.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCaller2003Men_7-7"><a href="#cite_note-MCaller2003Men-7">[7]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-DDatabase2003Men_8-2"><a href="#cite_note-DDatabase2003Men-8">[8]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes_9-4"><a href="#cite_note-BBCMensResults&amp;Prizes-9">[9]</a></sup>

</td><td rowspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-color:#aaa;border-style:solid;border-top-width:1px;border-left-width:1px;border-right-width:1px;border-bottom-width:1px;background-color:#f9f9f9"><b>3</b>

<h3><span id="Women.27s_draw"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Women's_draw">Women's draw</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2003_BDO_World_Darts_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Women's draw">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Numbers given to the left of players' names show the seedings for the top eight players in the women's competition. The three qualifiers are indicated by a (Q). The figures in brackets to the right of a competitor's name state their three-dart finishing averages in a match. Players in bold denote match winners.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MCallerWomen_49-4"><a href="#cite_note-MCallerWomen-49">[49]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BBCWomenResults_50-3"><a href="#cite_note-BBCWomenResults-50">[50]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54"><a href="#cite_note-54">[54]</a></sup>
</p>
